NOT wired into production simulator.\n\nDesign (Cengiz et al. 2019, QJE)\n---------------------------------\nBin the wage distribution (normalized to current MW) before and after\neach reform. Compare employment counts in three regions:\n\n  Below MW      : wage_ratio in [0.5, 1.0)  — missing mass post-reform\n  Affected      : wage_ratio in [0.9, 1.1)  — disemployment + bunching\n  Control       : wage_ratio in [1.3, 1.8)  — unaffected higher-wage jobs\n\nLocal elasticity  : ΔlnE_affected / Δln(MW)\nNet elasticity    : (ΔlnE_affected − ΔlnE_control) / Δln(MW)\n\nBoth panels normalized to their own contemporaneous MW (Cengiz convention):\n  pre  → wage_ratio = nom_wage / old_min\n  post → wage_ratio = nom_wage / new_min\n\nQuality gate\n------------\nNet elasticity in [-0.40, 0.10] AND bootstrap SE ≤ 0.20 → "ok"\nLocal only in range → "ok_local_only"\nOtherwise → "not_identified"\n\nUsage\n-----\n    python scripts/wage_bin_did.py [--skip-download] [--n-boot 500]\n')
